posted:Posted May 27, 2024
msg:The hotel environment is very good, with green trees, birds singing and insects chirping. You can see the Yulong River from the balcony, and you can see many bamboo rafts floating on the river every day. It takes 5 minutes to get to Jiefang Bridge. There are many tourists watching the sunset on the bridge. It is also very convenient to rent a battery car nearby, 30 yuan a day. The room is large, the breakfast has a variety of varieties and tastes good. For dinner, it is recommended to eat the farmhouse dishes at the door for economical and delicious. It is about 15 minutes by car from Yangshuo West Street. The hotel shuttle bus is scheduled and fixed, so this section of transportation is not very convenient, especially for us elderly people with poor legs and feet. The short shuttle from the West Street Cruise Terminal to the hotel cost nearly 70 for 4 people (15 yuan per person for the scenic area battery car + 8 yuan for Didi taxi).

The hotel is picturesque, surrounded by mountains and rivers, very much in the style of Southeast Asian hotels. We stayed in a river-view king-bed room, where we can see lush greenery, and we can see the bamboo rafts passing slowly on the Yulong River. Overlooking the rolling hills, the scenery is beautiful.

The location of the hotel is extremely superior. It is only a few minutes' walk to the pier where you can take the bamboo raft next to the Gongnong Bridge. You can rent a battery car when you turn right when you go out of the hotel. The hotel also has buses to and from West Street.

Service: The hotel waiter is a very shy young man, very nice, very enthusiastic to help us carry our luggage, and patiently explain the hotel's facilities and services to us. Because we came back late at West Street that night, the master waited patiently for us for an hour, thank you very much! In short, this hotel is very good in all aspects, and I will choose the Riverside Resort Hotel next time I come to Yangshuo!
